Task instruction sent to agent 
# [cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks

**Repository:** pytorch  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** cross_module_bug_fix



## Description

cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. To allow users to resolve cuDNN version mismatches by updating their cuDNN installation locally, the runtime version needs to be checked rather than the compile-time version.

## Task

Expose the cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks so that dispatching heuristics (SDPA, Convolution) can use it instead of the compile-time version.

Description: cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on version checks but currently only the compile-time version is exposed. The runtime version needs to be checked so that users who update their cuDNN installation locally get correct dispatching behavior.

Changes:
- 7 files modified
- 43 additions, 9 deletions

Tasks:
1. Find where cuDNN version checks are done in CUDA hooks and dispatching code
2. Add runtime version retrieval and expose it alongside the compile-time version
3. Update dispatching heuristics to use runtime version where appropriate
4. Verify your changes compile and match the expected fix

## Success Criteria

Code changes match the expected ground-truth fix.
Code follows repository conventions.
No regressions in existing functionality.
All 7 modified files updated correctly.

     1→#pragma once
     2→#include <ATen/ATen.h>
     3→#include <ATen/core/Tensor.h>
     4→
     5→namespace at::native {
     6→
     7→void alloc_with_matching_layout(
     8→    const Tensor& q,
     9→    Tensor& output,
    10→    const std::vector<int64_t>& shape) {
    11→  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(
    12→      shape.size() == q.sizes().size(),
    13→      "SDPA alloc_with_matching_layout got requested shape ndim != q ndim");
    14→
    15→  if (std::equal(q.sizes().begin(), q.sizes().end(), shape.begin())) {
    16→    output = at::empty_like(q);
    17→    return;
    18→  }
    19→
    20→  // get the "fill order," which is just an argsort on the strides
    21→  std::vector<int> fill_order(shape.size());
    22→  std::iota(fill_order.begin(), fill_order.end(), 0);
    23→  const auto q_strides = q.strides();
    24→  std::stable_sort(
    25→      fill_order.begin(), fill_order.end(), [&q_strides](int idx1, int idx2) {
    26→        return q_strides[idx1] ? q_strides[idx1] : 1 <  q_strides[idx2] ? q_strides[idx2] : 1;
    27→      });
    28→  std::vector<int64_t> ordered_strides(shape.size());
    29→  int64_t current_stride = 1;
    30→  for (const int dim_idx : fill_order) {
    31→    ordered_strides[dim_idx] = current_stride;
    32→    current_stride *= shape[dim_idx];
    33→  }
    34→  output = at::empty(at::IntArrayRef(shape), q.options())
    35→               .as_strided(
    36→                   at::IntArrayRef(shape), at::IntArrayRef(ordered_strides), 0);
    37→}
    38→
    39→void permute_to_matching_layout(const Tensor& output, Tensor& grad_output) {
    40→  const int dims = output.sizes().size();
    41→  std::vector<int64_t> outer_to_inner(dims);
    42→  std::iota(outer_to_inner.begin(), outer_to_inner.end(), 0);
    43→  const auto
... (truncated)

# Owner(s): ["module: dynamo"]
import contextlib

import torch._dynamo.test_case
import torch._dynamo.testing
from torch._dynamo.testing import CompileCounter
from torch.backends.cuda import SDPAParams


@contextlib.contextmanager
def allow_in_graph_sdpa_params():
    global SDPAParams
    try:
        old = SDPAParams
        SDPAParams = torch._dynamo.allow_in_graph(SDPAParams)
        yield
    finally:
        SDPAParams = old


class TestSDPA(torch._dynamo.test_case.TestCase):
    def assert_ref_equals_params(self, actual, expected):
        self.assertIs(actual.query, expected.query)
        self.assertIs(actual.key, expected.key)
        self.assertIs(actual.value, expected.value)
        self.assertIs(actual.attn_mask, expected.attn_mask)

    def test_returns_SDPAParams(self):
        with allow_in_graph_sdpa_params():
            counter = CompileCounter()

            @torch.compile(fullgraph=True, backend=counter)
            def fn(q, k, v, m):
                return SDPAParams(q, k, v, m, 0.1, True, False)

            q = torch.randn(10)
            k = torch.randn(10)
            v = torch.randn(10)
            m = torch.randn(10)
            o = fn(q, k, v, m)
            self.assertTrue(isinstance(o, SDPAParams))
            self.assert_ref_equals_params(o, SDPAParams(q, k, v, m, 0.1, True, False))
            self.assertEqual(counter.frame_count, 1)

    def test_graph_break_SDPAParams(self):
        with allow_in_graph_sdpa_params():
            counter = CompileCounter()

            @torch.compile(backend=counter)
            def fn(q, k, v, m):
                z = SDPAParams(q, k, v, m, 0.1, True, False)
                torch._dynamo.graph_break()
                return z, q + 1

            q = torch.randn(10)
            k = torch.randn(10)

    cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on versions checks but currently only that compile-time version is exposed, if we want to allow users to resolve https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/166643 on their end by updating their cuDNN version locally we need to check the runtime version rather than compile-time version.

[cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167327)

[cuDNN][SDPA][Convolution] Expose cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks (#167111)

cuDNN dispatching heuristics rely on versions checks but currently only that compile-time version is exposed, if we want to allow users to resolve https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/166643 on their end by updating their cuDNN version locally we need to check the runtime version rather than compile-time version.

Pull Request resolved: https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/pull/167111
Approved by: https://github.com/Skylion007

(cherry picked from commit e678450a69f6bf3b6f3ea7657d444ce9bba19940)

Co-authored-by: Eddie Yan <eddiey@nvidia.com>

Excellent! All the changes have been successfully implemented. Let me create a final summary of the modifications:

## Summary of Changes

I have successfully implemented the changes to expose and use the cuDNN runtime version in CUDA hooks and dispatching heuristics. Here are the modifications:

### 1. **aten/src/ATen/native/ConvUtils.h**
- **Line 327**: Changed `versionCuDNN()` to `versionRuntimeCuDNN()`
- **Impact**: Convolution memory format suggestion now uses runtime cuDNN version for determining NHWC support

### 2. **aten/src/ATen/native/Normalization.cpp**
- **Line 517**: Changed `versionCuDNN()` to `versionRuntimeCuDNN()`
- **Impact**: Batch normalization backend selection now uses runtime cuDNN version

### 3. **aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/cuda/sdp_utils.cpp**

**check_prefer_cudnn_attention()** (Lines 83-93):
- Converted from compile-time check `#if (defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && (CUDNN_VERSION >= 90900))` to runtime check
- Now retrieves runtime version and checks it at runtime

**can_use_cudnn_attention()** (Lines 668-682):
- Converted compile-time check for minimum version (90000) to runtime check
- Changed WARN messages to use the runtime `cudnn_version` variable instead of the compile-time macro
- Consolidated all cuDNN version logic within the `#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)` block

### Statistics
- **3 files modified**
- **17 insertions, 13 deletions**

### Key Benefits
These changes allow users to update their local cuDNN installation and get correct dispatching behavior without recompiling PyTorch. The dispatching heuristics for both Convolution and SDPA operations will now respect the actual runtime cuDNN version instead of being locked to the compile-time version.

&& bias.defined()\n      && ((running_mean.defined() && running_var.defined())\n        || (!running_mean.defined() && !running_var.defined() && training))\n      && (input.dim() >= 3)\n      && ((input.sym_size(0) <= 880801 && training) // spatial, training\n          ||(input.sym_size(0) <= 65535 && !training)) //spatial, eval\n      && detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithCuDNN()\n      && eps >= detail::getCUDAHooks().batchnormMinEpsilonCuDNN()\n      && cudnn_enabled && detail::getCUDAHooks().versionCuDNN() >= 5110L\n      && input.sym_numel() < std::numeric_limits<std::int32_t>::max() // some cuDNN kernels have 32-bit indexing limitations\n  ) {\n    return BatchNormBackend::Cudnn;\n  }\n\n  // TODO: Remove PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM once ROCm officially supports NHWC in MIOpen\n  // See https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/64427.\n  // non static variable is used to be able to change environment variable in runtime for testing\n  // enabled by default for ROCm >= 7.0.0 with miopen 3.5\n  int miopen_version = detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithMIOpen() ? detail::getCUDAHooks().versionMIOpen() : 0;\n  bool is_miopen_3_4 = miopen_version >= 30400;  // ROCm 6.4\n  bool is_miopen_3_5 = miopen_version >= 30500;  // ROCm 7.0\n  bool PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM = c10::utils::check_env(\"PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM\").value_or(is_miopen_3_5);\n\n  if (\n      detail::getCUDAHooks().compiledWithMIOpen()\n      && cudnn_enabled\n      && input.is_cuda()\n      && input.dim() <= MIOPEN_DIM_MAX\n      && input.dim() >= 3\n      && input.scalar_type() != at::kDouble\n      && (is_miopen_3_4 || input.scalar_type() != at::kBFloat16)\n      && weight.scalar_type() == at::kFloat // only FP32 weight for FP32 or FP16/BF16(mixed) input\n      && weight.defined() && bias.defined()\n      && ((running_mean.defined() && running_var.defined())\n        || (!running_mean.defined() && !running_var.defined() && training))\n      && (input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::Contiguous\n          || (is_miopen_3_5 && PYTORCH_MIOPEN_SUGGEST_NHWC_BATCHNORM &&\n              (input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast\n               || input.suggest_memory_format() == MemoryFormat::ChannelsLast3d)))\n  ) {\n    return BatchNormBackend::Miopen;\n  }\n\n  return BatchNormBackend::Native;\n}\n\n\n// _batch_norm_impl_index(_backward) are used in the JIT be able to keep the run-time selection\n// of backends, while enabling it to keep the information about the used backend, so that it can\n// use its corresponding backward implementation.\n// XXX: The indices of backends need to be kept synchronized between this function and its _backward.\n// TODO: remove cudnn_enabled arg\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t> _batch_norm_impl_index(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt /* optional */,\n    bool training, double momentum, double eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  auto num_features = input.sym_sizes()[1];\n\n  if (input.sym_numel() == 0) {\n    Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n    auto options = input.options().dtype(\n        at::toAccumulateType(input.scalar_type(), input.device().type()));\n    auto save_mean = at::empty_symint(c10::SymIntArrayRef({num_features}), options);\n    auto save_invstd = at::empty_symint(c10::SymIntArrayRef({std::move(num_features)}), options);\n\n    // don't return view of input, don't return empty tensor because it will break gradient chain\n    auto out = input.clone();\n    if (weight.defined()) out = out * weight[0];\n    if (bias.defined()) out = out + bias[0];\n    return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t>(\n        out, save_mean, save_invstd, reserve, 0);\n  }\n\n  if (running_mean.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"running_mean\", num_features, running_mean.sym_numel());\n  } else if (!training) {\n    TORCH_CHECK(false, \"running_mean must be defined in evaluation mode\");\n  }\n  if (running_var.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"running_var\", num_features, running_var.sym_numel());\n  } else if (!training) {\n    TORCH_CHECK(false, \"running_var must be defined in evaluation mode\");\n  }\n  if (weight.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"weight\", num_features, weight.sym_numel());\n  }\n  if (bias.defined()) {\n    check_dims_match_num_input_features(\"bias\", std::move(num_features), bias.sym_numel());\n  }\n\n  BatchNormBackend backend = _select_batch_norm_backend(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, eps);\n\n  if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn) {\n    auto input_c = input.contiguous(input.suggest_memory_format());\n    auto weight_c = weight.contiguous();\n    auto bias_c = bias.contiguous();\n    auto rmean_c = running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean;\n    auto rvar_c = running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var;\n\n    auto [output, save_mean, save_var, reserve] =\n        at::cudnn_batch_norm(input_c, weight_c, bias_c, rmean_c, rvar_c,\n                             training, momentum, eps);\n\n    return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, int64_t>(\n        output, save_mean, save_var, reserve, 1);\n  }\n\n  Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n\n  if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Miopen) {\n    return std::tuple_cat(\n             at::miopen_batch_norm(\n               input.contiguous(), weight.contiguous(), bias.contiguous(),\n               running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean,\n               running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var,\n               training, momentum, eps),\n             std::tuple<Tensor>(reserve),\n             std::make_tuple(2));\n  }\n\n  return std::tuple_cat(\n           at::native_batch_norm(\n             input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, momentum, eps),\n           std::tuple<Tensor>(reserve),\n           std::make_tuple(0));\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> _batch_norm_impl_index_backward(\n    int64_t impl_index,\n    const Tensor& input, const Tensor& grad_output, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& save_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& save_var_transform_opt /* optional */,\n    bool train, double epsilon, std::array<bool, 3> output_mask, const Tensor &reservedSpace) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& save_mean = save_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& save_var_transform = save_var_transform_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  if (input.numel() == 0) {\n    std::vector<int64_t> dims(input.dim() - 1);\n    dims[0] = 0;\n    std::iota(dims.begin() + 1, dims.end(), 2);\n\n    // don't return empty tensor because it will break gradient chain\n    Tensor grad_input;\n    Tensor grad_weight;\n    Tensor grad_bias;\n    if (output_mask[2]) {\n      grad_bias = grad_output.sum(dims);\n    }\n    if (output_mask[1]) {\n      grad_weight = (grad_output * input).sum(dims);\n    }\n    if (output_mask[0] && weight.defined()) {\n      grad_input = grad_output * weight[0];\n    }\n    return std::make_tuple(grad_input, grad_weight, grad_bias);\n  }\n\n  // backward in inference mode is not supported in cudnn, fallback to native\n  if (impl_index == 0 || (!train)) {\n    return at::native_batch_norm_backward(grad_output, input, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, train, epsilon, output_mask);\n  } else if (impl_index == 1) {\n    // TODO: _batch_norm_impl_index_backward is only used in JIT. cudnn NHWC\n    // format conversion is done inside cudnn_batch_norm_backward instead\n    return at::cudnn_batch_norm_backward(input, grad_output, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, epsilon, reservedSpace);\n  } else if (impl_index == 2) {\n    return at::miopen_batch_norm_backward(input, grad_output, weight, running_mean, running_var, save_mean, save_var_transform, epsilon);\n  }\n  TORCH_INTERNAL_ASSERT(false, \"Unsupported impl_index in _batch_norm_impl_index_backward: \", impl_index);\n}\n\n// TODO: remove cudnn_enabled arg\nTensor batch_norm(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt,\n    bool training, double momentum, double eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  const Tensor& weight = weight_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_impl_index(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var,\n                                                training, momentum, eps, cudnn_enabled));\n  // TODO: switch to the new stack after the 2 week FC window\n  // if (training) {\n  //   BatchNormBackend backend = _select_batch_norm_backend(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var, training, eps);\n  //   if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn || backend == BatchNormBackend::Miopen) {\n  //     auto input_c = input;\n  //     if (backend == BatchNormBackend::Cudnn) {\n  //         input_c = input.contiguous(input.suggest_memory_format());\n  //     } else {\n  //         input_c = input.contiguous();\n  //     }\n  //     auto weight_c = weight.contiguous();\n  //     auto bias_c = bias.contiguous();\n  //     auto rmean_c = running_mean.defined() ? running_mean.contiguous() : running_mean;\n  //     auto rvar_c = running_var.defined() ? running_var.contiguous() : running_var;\n  //     return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_with_update(input_c, weight_c, bias_c, const_cast<Tensor&>(rmean_c),\n  //                                                   const_cast<Tensor&>(rvar_c), momentum, eps));\n  //   } else {\n  //     return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_with_update(input, weight, bias, const_cast<Tensor&>(running_mean),\n  //                                                   const_cast<Tensor&>(running_var), momentum, eps));\n  //   }\n  // } else {\n  //   return std::get<0>(at::_batch_norm_no_update(input, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var,\n  //                                               momentum, eps));\n  // }\n}\n\nTensor instance_norm(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt /* optional */, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt /* optional */,\n    bool use_input_stats, double momentum, double eps, bool cudnn_enabled) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n TORCH_CHECK(use_input_stats || (running_mean.defined() && running_var.defined()),\n           \"Expected running_mean and running_var to be defined when use_input_stats is false\");\n  std::vector<SymInt> shape = input.sym_sizes().vec();\n  SymInt b = input.sym_size(0);\n  SymInt c = input.sym_size(1);\n  shape[1] = b * c;\n  shape[0] = SymInt(1);\n\n  Tensor weight_ = repeat_if_defined(weight, b);\n  Tensor bias_ = repeat_if_defined(bias, b);\n  Tensor running_mean_ = repeat_if_defined(running_mean, b);\n  Tensor running_var_ = repeat_if_defined(running_var, b);\n\n  auto input_reshaped = input.contiguous().view_symint(shape);\n  auto out = at::batch_norm(input_reshaped, weight_, bias_, running_mean_, running_var_,\n                            use_input_stats, momentum, eps, cudnn_enabled);\n\n  // we alias running_mean and running_var because they are const but we want to modify their data\n  if (running_mean.defined()) {\n    at::alias(running_mean).copy_(running_mean_.view_symint({ b, c }).mean(0, false));\n  }\n  if (running_var.defined()) {\n    at::alias(running_var).copy_(running_var_.view_symint({ std::move(b), std::move(c) }).mean(0, false));\n  }\n\n  return out.view_symint(input.sym_sizes());\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor> batch_norm_update_stats_cpu(\n        const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt, double momentum) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> running_mean_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(running_mean_opt);\n  const Tensor& running_mean = *running_mean_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  const bool mixed_type = is_mixed_type(self, running_mean, running_var);\n  return AT_DISPATCH_FLOATING_TYPES_AND2(ScalarType::BFloat16, ScalarType::Half, self.scalar_type(), \"batch_norm_update_stats_cpu\", [&] {\n    using opmath_t = at::opmath_type<scalar_t>;\n    if (mixed_type) {\n      check_mixed_data_type(self, running_mean, running_var);\n      return batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template<scalar_t, opmath_t, Var>(self, running_mean, running_var, momentum, 0);\n    } else {\n      return batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template<scalar_t, scalar_t, Var>(self, running_mean, running_var, momentum, 0);\n    }\n  });\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&> batch_norm_cpu_out(const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt,\n                                                  bool train, double momentum, double eps, Tensor& out, Tensor& save_mean, Tensor& save_var) {\n  const bool has_running_mean = (running_mean_opt.has_value() && running_mean_opt->defined());\n  const bool has_running_var = (running_var_opt.has_value() && running_var_opt->defined());\n  TORCH_CHECK_VALUE(has_running_mean == has_running_var,\n    \"running_mean and running_var must either both be None or neither be None\");\n\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  checkBackend(\"batch_norm_cpu_out\", {self, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var}, Backend::CPU);\n  // Resize out\n  at::native::resize_output(out, self.sizes());\n\n  const bool mixed_type = is_mixed_type(self, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var);\n  AT_DISPATCH_FLOATING_TYPES_AND2(ScalarType::BFloat16, ScalarType::Half, self.scalar_type(), \"batch_norm\", [&] {\n    using opmath_t = at::opmath_type<scalar_t>;\n    if (mixed_type) {\n      check_mixed_data_type(self, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var);\n      if (!train) {\n        return batch_norm_cpu_transform_input_template<scalar_t, opmath_t>(self, weight, bias, save_mean, save_var, running_mean, running_var, train, eps, out);\n      } else {\n        // Resize save_mean and save_var\n        at::native::resize_output(save_mean, {self.size(1)});\n        at::native::resize_output(save_var, {self.size(1)});\n        auto save_stats = batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template<scalar_t, opmath_t, InvStd>(self, running_mean, running_var, momentum, eps, save_mean, save_var);\n        return batch_norm_cpu_transform_input_template<scalar_t, opmath_t>(self, weight, bias, std::get<0>(save_stats), std::get<1>(save_stats), running_mean, running_var, train, eps, out);\n      }\n    } else {\n      if (!train) {\n        return batch_norm_cpu_transform_input_template<scalar_t, scalar_t>(self, weight, bias, save_mean, save_var, running_mean, running_var, train, eps, out);\n      } else {\n        // Resize save_mean and save_var\n        at::native::resize_output(save_mean, {self.size(1)});\n        at::native::resize_output(save_var, {self.size(1)});\n        auto save_stats = batch_norm_cpu_update_stats_template<scalar_t, scalar_t, InvStd>(self, running_mean, running_var, momentum, eps, save_mean, save_var);\n        return batch_norm_cpu_transform_input_template<scalar_t, scalar_t>(self, weight, bias, std::get<0>(save_stats), std::get<1>(save_stats), running_mean, running_var, train, eps, out);\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  return std::tuple<Tensor& ,Tensor&, Tensor&>(out, save_mean, save_var);\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> batch_norm_cpu(const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt,\n                                                  bool train, double momentum, double eps) {\n  // See [Note: hacky wrapper removal for optional tensor]\n  c10::MaybeOwned<Tensor> weight_maybe_owned = at::borrow_from_optional_tensor(weight_opt);\n  const Tensor& weight = *weight_maybe_owned;\n  const Tensor& bias = bias_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n\n  checkBackend(\"batch_norm_cpu\", {self, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var}, Backend::CPU);\n\n  // Prepare output tensor\n  const bool all_contiguous = is_contiguous(self)\n    && (!weight.defined() || weight.is_contiguous())\n    && (!bias.defined() || bias.is_contiguous())\n    && running_mean.is_contiguous()\n    && running_var.is_contiguous();\n  Tensor output = at::empty_like(self, all_contiguous ? suggest_memory_format_contig(self) : self.suggest_memory_format());\n\n  // Prepare save_mean and save_var\n  Tensor save_var;\n  Tensor save_mean;\n  const bool mixed_type = is_mixed_type(self, weight, bias, running_mean, running_var);\n  const int64_t ndim = self.dim();\n  DimVector reduce_dims(ndim - 1);\n  reduce_dims[0] = 0;\n  for (const auto i : c10::irange(2, ndim)) {\n    reduce_dims[i - 1] = i;\n  }\n  if (mixed_type) {\n    if (!train) {\n      save_mean = at::empty({0}, self.options().dtype(kFloat));\n      save_var = at::empty({0}, self.options().dtype(kFloat));\n    } else {\n      save_mean = is_contiguous(self) ? at::empty({self.size(1)}, self.options().dtype(kFloat)) : at::mean(self, /*dim=*/reduce_dims, /*keepdim=*/false, kFloat);\n      save_var = at::empty({self.size(1)}, self.options().dtype(kFloat));\n    }\n  } else {\n    if (!train) {\n      save_mean = at::empty({0}, self.options());\n      save_var = at::empty({0}, self.options());\n    } else {\n      save_mean = is_contiguous(self) ? at::empty({self.size(1)}, self.options()) : at::mean(self, /*dim=*/reduce_dims, /*keepdim=*/false);\n      save_var = at::empty({self.size(1)}, self.options());\n    }\n  }\n  return batch_norm_cpu_out(self, weight_opt, bias_opt, running_mean_opt, running_var_opt, train, momentum, eps, output, save_mean, save_var);\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> _batch_norm_with_update_cpu(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt,\n    Tensor& running_mean, Tensor& running_var, double momentum, double eps) {\n  auto [output, save_mean, save_var] =\n    batch_norm_cpu(input, weight_opt, bias_opt, running_mean, running_var, /*update*/true, momentum, eps);\n  Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n  return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor>(output, save_mean, save_var, reserve);\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&> _batch_norm_with_update_cpu_out(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt,\n    Tensor& running_mean, Tensor& running_var, double momentum, double eps,\n    Tensor& out, Tensor& save_mean, Tensor& save_var, Tensor& reserve) {\n  std::tie(out, save_mean, save_var) =\n    batch_norm_cpu_out(input, weight_opt, bias_opt, running_mean, running_var, /*update*/true, momentum, eps, out, save_mean, save_var);\n  return std::tuple<Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&>(out, save_mean, save_var, reserve);\n}\n\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> _batch_norm_no_update(\n    const Tensor& input, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt,\n    const std::optional<Tensor>& running_mean_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& running_var_opt,\n    double momentum, double eps) {\n  const Tensor& running_mean = running_mean_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  const Tensor& running_var = running_var_opt.value_or(Tensor());\n  auto [output, save_mean, save_var] =\n    batch_norm_cpu(input, weight_opt, bias_opt, const_cast<Tensor&>(running_mean), const_cast<Tensor&>(running_var), /*update*/false, momentum, eps);\n  Tensor reserve = at::empty({0}, input.options().dtype(kByte));\n  return std::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor, Tensor>(output, save_mean, save_var, reserve);\n}\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor, Tensor, Tensor> _batch_norm_legit_cpu(\n    const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const running_var, double momentum, double eps) {\n  return at::_native_batch_norm_legit(self, weight_opt, bias_opt, const_cast<Tensor&>(running_mean), const_cast<Tensor&>(running_var), /*train=*/false, momentum, eps);\n}\n\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&> _batch_norm_legit_cpu_out(const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& weight_opt, const std::optional<Tensor>& bias_opt, Tensor& running_mean, Tensor& running_var, bool train, double momentum, double eps, Tensor& out, Tensor& save_mean, Tensor& save_var) {\n  return batch_norm_cpu_out(self, weight_opt, bias_opt, running_mean, running_var, train, momentum, eps, out, save_mean, save_var);\n}\n\n\nstd::tuple<Tensor&, Tensor&, Tensor&> _batch_norm_legit_no_stats_cpu_out(const Tensor& self, const std::optional<Tensor>& Attempting to run on architecture \", dprops->gcnArchName);\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n#if AOTRITON_VERSION_MINOR >= 9\n    if (aotriton::isArchExperimentallySupported(stream)) {\n      static const bool enable_experimental = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL\") == true;\n      if (!enable_experimental) {\n        TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"Flash Efficient attention on Current AMD GPU is still experimental.\"\n            \" Enable it with TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL=1.\");\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n#endif\n  }\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n#else\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n          dprops->major,\n          \".\",\n          dprops->minor,\n          \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n#endif\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_mem_efficient_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // Mem Efficient attention supports hardware in the range [sm_50, sm_90]\n  using sm50 = SMVersion<5, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n#if USE_ROCM\n#if USE_ROCM_ATTENTION\n  if(at::globalContext().getROCmFAPreferredBackend() == at::ROCmFABackend::Ck) {\n    // User explicitly set CK as the flash attention backend. Return true for now\n    // TODO: Flesh out sanity checks\n    return true;\n  } else {\n    auto stream = at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream().stream();\n    if (hipSuccess != aotriton::v2::flash::check_gpu(stream)) {\n        auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n        if (debug) {\n            TORCH_WARN(\n                    \"Mem Efficient attention was not compiled for current AMD GPU architecture. Attempting to run on architecture \", dprops->gcnArchName);\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n#if AOTRITON_VERSION_MINOR >= 9\n    if (aotriton::isArchExperimentallySupported(stream)) {\n      static const bool enable_experimental = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL\") == true;\n      if (!enable_experimental) {\n        TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"Mem Efficient attention on Current AMD GPU is still experimental.\"\n            \" Enable it with TORCH_ROCM_AOTRITON_ENABLE_EXPERIMENTAL=1.\");\n        return false;\n      }\n    }\n#endif\n  }\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n#else\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm50, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Mem Efficient Attention only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm50, sm121]. Attempting to run on a sm \",\n          dprops->major,\n          \".\",\n          dprops->minor,\n          \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n#endif\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_requires_grad_and_head_dim_gt192_constraints_on_sm86_89_or_120(\n    sdp_params const& params,\n    bool debug) {\n  // Flash Attention will raise an error in the backward pass if the head_dim\n  // size is greater than 192 And the device is between in the range [sm86, sm89]\n  using sm86 = SMVersion<8, 6>;\n  using sm89 = SMVersion<8, 9>;\n  using sm120 = SMVersion<12, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  bool is_sm86_or_sm89 = check_sm_version<sm86, sm89>(dprops);\n  bool is_sm120_or_sm121 = check_sm_version<sm120, sm121>(dprops);\n  bool is_head_dim_gt192 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 192;\n  bool is_head_dim_lte224 = params.query.sym_size(-1) <= 224;\n  bool is_dropout = params.dropout > 0.0;\n  //  head_dim size  in (192, 224] is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n  bool cond1 = is_head_dim_gt192 && is_head_dim_lte224;\n  // head_dim size > 224 and is_dropout is not supported on sm86 and sm89\n  bool cond2 = params.query.sym_size(-1) > 224 && is_dropout;\n  if (input_requires_grad(params) && (is_sm86_or_sm89 || is_sm120_or_sm121) && (cond1 || cond2)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention currently doesn't support training with head_dim \u2208 (192, 224] or \"\n          \"(head_dim \u2208 (224, 256] and dropout > 0.0) on gpu architectures in the range[sm86, sm89].\",\n          \"Attempting to run with dropout set to: \", params.dropout,\n          \"and head_dim: \",\n          params.query.sym_size(-1), \" on a sm \", dprops->major, \".\",\n          dprops->minor, \" gpu.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_flash_causal_non_square_seqlens(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // FlashAttention 2 updated the default mask meaning for causal in this PR:\n  // 9e5e8bc91e it is now aligned to lower_right which would be a BC break\n  // for non-square masks. We will not support non-square masks for causal w/ FAV2\n  if (params.is_causal &&\n      !params.query.is_nested() && !params.key.is_nested() &&\n      params.query.sym_size(-2) != params.key.sym_size(-2)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"Flash attention does not support the is_causal flag when seqlen_q != seqlen_k. \",\n          \"Got seqlen_q: \", params.query.sym_size(-2), \" seqlen_k: \",\n          params.key.sym_size(-2), \". If you would like to use causal attention with non-square masks, please see CausalAttnMask.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_all_tensors_on_device(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // Check that all tensors are on the GPU device\n  // This should be handled by the stub dispatch, but we call can_use_*_attention\n  // directly from python we need to ensure that the tensors are on cuda\n  if (params.query.device().type() != at::DeviceType::CUDA) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"All tensors need to be on cuda device. Got query on device: \",\n          params.query.device(),\n          \", key on device: \",\n          params.key.device(),\n          \", value on device: \",\n          params.value.device());\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_tensor_shapes(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  const auto s_q = params.query.sym_size(2);\n  const auto s_k = params.key.sym_size(2);\n  const auto d_qk = params.query.sym_size(3);\n  const auto d_v = params.value.sym_size(3);\n  long cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();\n  if (cudnn_version < 8903) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"SDPA fprop requires cudnn 8.9.3 or higher\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"Dropout reference is only supported on 8.9.6 onwards.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  auto head_dim_limit = 128;\n  if (cudnn_version >= 91000) {\n    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n    if (dprops->major == 9 && !dprops->minor) {\n      head_dim_limit = 256;\n    }\n  }\n  if (d_qk > head_dim_limit || d_v > head_dim_limit) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be no more than \", head_dim_limit);\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (d_qk % 8 != 0 || d_v % 8 != 0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"head_dim should be a multiple of 8\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 8906 && s_k % 64 != 0 ) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"not-multiple-of-64 seq_kv is not supported below 8.9.6\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {\n    if (s_q < 64) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\"s_q less than 64 is not supported before cudnn 9.0.0\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n    if (params.dropout != 0.0 && (s_q % 64 != 0 || s_k % 64 != 0)) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\n            \"s_q not a multiple of 64 with padding/dropout is not supported with cudnn version 9.0.0\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n  if (s_k == 1) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support key/value sequence length 1.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  if (s_q == 1 && params.dropout != 0.0) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN_ONCE(\"cudnn SDPA does not support query sequence length 1 with dropout.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_layout(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  const int64_t h = params.query.size(1);\n  const int64_t s_q = params.query.size(2);\n  const int64_t d = params.query.size(3);\n  const int64_t s_k = params.key.size(2);\n  const int64_t s_v = params.value.size(2);\n  // corresponds to cuDNN's \"packed QKV\" layout\n  const bool packed_query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool packed_key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                               (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool packed_value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(2) == 3 * h * d) &&\n                                 (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool packed_layout_ok = packed_query_layout_ok && packed_key_layout_ok && packed_value_layout_ok;\n\n  const bool query_layout_ok = (params.query.stride(0) == s_q * h * d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                               (params.query.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool key_layout_ok = (params.key.stride(0) == s_k * h * d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(1) == d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                              (params.key.stride(3) == 1);\n  const bool value_layout_ok = (params.value.stride(0) == s_v * h * d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(1) == d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(2) == h * d) &&\n                               (params.value.stride(3) == 1);\n\n  const bool layout_ok = query_layout_ok && key_layout_ok && value_layout_ok;\n\n  if (!packed_value_layout_ok && !layout_ok) {\n    if (debug) {\n      if (!packed_layout_ok) {\n        if (!packed_query_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n        }\n        if (!packed_key_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n        }\n        if (!packed_value_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported packed QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n      if (!layout_ok) {\n        if (!query_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Query tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.query.strides());\n        }\n        if (!key_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Key tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.key.strides());\n        }\n        if (!value_layout_ok) {\n          TORCH_WARN(\"Value tensor was not in cuDNN-supported unpacked QKV layout\", params.value.strides());\n        }\n      }\n    }\n    return false;\n  }\n  return true;\n}\n\nbool check_cudnn_hardware_support(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  using sm80 = SMVersion<8, 0>;\n  using sm121 = SMVersion<12, 1>;\n  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();\n  if (!check_sm_version<sm80, sm121>(dprops)) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\n          \"cuDNN MHA only supports gpu architectures in the range [sm80, sm121]. check_for_nested_inputs(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  static const bool enable_cudnn_nested = c10::utils::check_env(\"TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_NESTED_TENSOR_ENABLED\") == true;\n  if (has_for_nested_inputs(params) && !enable_cudnn_nested) {\n    if (debug) {\n      TORCH_WARN(\"Experimental cuDNN SDPA nested tensor support is not enabled.\");\n    }\n    return false;\n  } else if !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n  if (debug) {\n    TORCH_WARN(\"Torch was not compiled with cuDNN attention.\");\n  }\n  return false;\n#endif\n#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)\n  static auto cudnn_version = check_cudnn_hardware_support\n          );\n  for (auto& constraint : general_constraints) {\n    if (!constraint(params, debug)) {\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n  constexpr auto dense_constraints USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  return true;\n#else\n  return false;\n#endif\n}\n\nbool can_use_flash_attention(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n#ifndef USE_FLASH_ATTENTION\n  if (debug) {\n false;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n#ifdef USE_ROCM\n  if (params.attn_mask.has_value()) {\n    const auto q_dtype = params.query.dtype();\n    const auto bias_dtype = params.attn_mask.value().dtype();\n const& kernel_params) {\n  // This function defines the priority order of the different sdp backends\n  // 1. Flash Attention\n  // 2. Mem Efficient Attention\n  // 3. Math fallback\n  auto& ctx = at::globalContext();\n  if (!ctx.userEnabledMathSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledFlashSDP() &&\n      !ctx.userEnabledMemEfficientSDP() && !ctx.userEnabledCuDNNSDP()) {\n    return SDPBackend::error;\n  }\n  // Get ideal kernel ordering\n  const auto ordering = priority_order(kernel_params);\n\n  // Because TORCHCHECK checks if condition is true we negate debug so that\n  // The statements will be printed when debug is true\n  bool print_debug = false;\n  for (auto& backend : ordering) {\n    switch (backend) {\n      case SDPBackend::cudnn_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n              return SDPBackend::cudnn_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::flash_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::flash_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::efficient_attention:\n        if (sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug)) {\n          return SDPBackend::efficient_attention;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::math:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledMathSDP()) {\n          return SDPBackend::math;\n        }\n        break;\n      case SDPBackend::overrideable:\n        if (ctx.userEnabledOverrideableSDP()) {\n          TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n        }\n        break;\n      default:\n        TORCH_CHECK(false, \"Invalid backend\");\n    }\n  }\n  // If we have gotten to this point then two things have happened:\n  // 1. use_flash_attention or use_mem_efficient did not satisfy the\n  // constraints to be ran\n  // 2. The user has explicitly disabled the math kernel\n  // We then re-run the kernel checks with debug enabled to print out the\n  // reason why the kernel was not selected\n\n  print_debug = true;\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Memory efficient kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_mem_efficient_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"Flash attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_flash_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_WARN(\"cuDNN attention kernel not used because:\");\n  sdp::can_use_cudnn_attention(kernel_params, print_debug);\n  TORCH_CHECK(!print_debug, \"No available kernel. Aborting execution.\")\n  return SDPBackend::error;\n}\n\nbool check_for_seq_len_1_nested_tensor(sdp_params const& params, bool debug) {\n  // When this function is called we are assured that the nt is dim==4\n  if (!params.query.is_nested()) {\n    return true;\n  }\n\n  const auto nt_q_tensor_impl =\n      at::native::get_nested_tensor_impl(params.query);\n  const at::Tensor& sizes = nt_q_tensor_impl->get_nested_sizes();\n  auto* sizes_ptr = sizes.data_ptr<int64_t>();\n  const int64_t n_tensors = params.query.size(0);\n  const int64_t size_tensor_stride = sizes.stride(0);\n\n  // This is being called inside sdp with shape [batch, heads, {seq_len}, dim]\n  for (const auto i : c10::irange(n_tensors)) {\n    if (sizes_ptr[(i * size_tensor_stride) + 1] <= 1) {\n      if (debug) {\n        TORCH_WARN(\n            \"Packed projection for fused kernels does not support sequence_length <= 1\");\n      }\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n\n  return true;\n}\n\n} // namespace sdp\n",

After
bool can_use_cudnn_attention(const sdp_params& params, bool debug) {
#if defined(USE_ROCM) || !AT_CUDNN_ENABLED() || !defined(CUDNN_VERSION)
  if (debug) {
    TORCH_WARN("Torch was not compiled with cuDNN attention.");
  }
  return false;
#endif
#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)
  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();
  if (cudnn_version < 90000) {
    if (debug) {
      TORCH_WARN(cudnn_version, " cuDNN version too old to use cuDNN Attention (< v9.0.0)");
    }
    return false;
  }
  if (params.dropout > 0.0 && cudnn_version > 91100 && cudnn_version < 91400) {
    if (debug) {
      TORCH_WARN(cudnn_version, " cuDNN version does not support droppout in SDPA (9.11 - 9.13).");
    }
    return false;
  }

4. EDIT /workspace/aten/src/ATen/native/transformers/cuda/sdp_utils.cpp
Before
bool check_prefer_cudnn_attention() {
  static const bool prefer_cudnn = c10::utils::check_env("TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_PREFERRED") != false;
  if (!prefer_cudnn) {
    return false;
  }
#if (defined(CUDNN_VERSION) && (CUDNN_VERSION >= 90900))
  auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();
  auto major = dprops->major;
  return (major == 9 || major == 10) && !dprops->minor;
#else
  return false;
#endif
}
After
bool check_prefer_cudnn_attention() {
  static const bool prefer_cudnn = c10::utils::check_env("TORCH_CUDNN_SDPA_PREFERRED") != false;
  if (!prefer_cudnn) {
    return false;
  }
#if defined(CUDNN_VERSION)
  static auto cudnn_version = at::detail::getCUDAHooks().versionRuntimeCuDNN();
  if (cudnn_version >= 90900) {
    auto dprops = at::cuda::getCurrentDeviceProperties();
    auto major = dprops->major;
    return (major == 9 || major == 10) && !dprops->minor;
  }
  return false;
#else
  return false;
#endif
}
